Composite index`[tenantId, brokerId, kind, verifiedAt]` provisioned for the two M7.6a aggregate queries (`sentimentAggregate WHERE kind=REVIEW`and`verifiedComplaintCount WHERE kind=COMPLAINT AND verifiedAt IS NOT NULL`). Migration `20260526034736_add_review_kind_discriminator`is`CREATE TYPE`+`ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN`6 lines +`CREATE INDEX`— no UPDATE statements.`packages/db/src/index.ts`adds`ReviewKind`to the alphabetised re-export. Both`packages/db`and`apps/api`typecheck green after`prisma generate`. **M7.2** (`39bf320`, 30 lines) `feat(api): add complaint outbox event vocabulary with ack-only handlers`—`apps/api/src/tasks/outbox-worker.ts`poll loop adds three explicit`else if`branches for`complaint.submitted`/`complaint.verified`/`complaint.rejected`matching the ack-only pattern previously used for`verification.broker_added`, suppressing the `Unknown event type`warn noise that would otherwise pollute the worker log when M7.3 starts emitting these events. Per ADR-0029 D7 Phase 1 doesn't put complaints on-chain so the handlers fall through to`processedAt`update without side effects; the file header docstring is updated to enumerate the three new event types and explicitly notes that`complaint.rejected`worker MUST NOT modify the Review row (rule 00「reject ≠ delete」 invariant — admin path already only mutates`adminNote`, but the doc puts the red line where the next worker maintainer reads first). **M7.3a** (`968fc0f`, 424 lines) `feat(api): bootstrap complaints domain types and Prisma repository`— atomic-but-large per the M5.1 / M6.0 / M6.2a precedent (three files type-circularly dependent — extracting them into separate commits leaves intermediate commits unable to compile). New`apps/api/src/domains/complaints/`directory with three files: (a)`domain/ComplaintEntity.ts`(116 lines) ships`SubmitComplaintInput`(required`evidenceIpfsCid`, optional `respondsToReviewId`, `kind: 'COMPLAINT'`literal carried through),`ComplaintRecord`(read-side projection mirroring`ReviewRecord`shape but with the complaint-specific fields surfaced), and a derived`ComplaintVerificationStatus = 'OPEN' | 'VERIFIED' | 'REJECTED'`— the public-facing status is **derived from`verifiedAt`+`adminNote`rather than persisted in a status column** per ADR-0029 D4 to keep`Review.status`(PENDING/CONFIRMED/FAILED) free for the on-chain pipeline that's reused for Phase 3 jury anchoring. (b)`domain/IComplaintRepository.ts`(82 lines) declares the port with`create`/`findById`/`list`/`applyVerification` — the verify/reject mutation parameter is a **discriminated union (`kind: 'verify' | 'reject'`) rather than two methods**, so the repository implementation can emit the correct outbox event in the same transaction and the rule-00 invariant ("verify branch never touches body / title / evidenceIpfsCid / contentHash / ipfsCid; reject branch only writes adminNote") is encoded into the type system rather than the docstring. (c) `infrastructure/PrismaComplaintRepository.ts`(229 lines) implements the port:`create`writes a`Review`row with`kind: 'COMPLAINT'`+ same-tx outbox`complaint.submitted`event (carries`complaintId`+`brokerSlug`+`userId`), `findById`includes a`kind = 'COMPLAINT'`guard so the repository never returns a review row by accident,`list`translates the derived`OPEN | VERIFIED | REJECTED | undefined`filter into the corresponding`verifiedAt IS NULL/NOT NULL`×`adminNote IS NULL/NOT NULL` boolean pair (`OPEN: verifiedAt IS NULL AND adminNote IS NULL`; `VERIFIED: verifiedAt IS NOT NULL`; `REJECTED: adminNote IS NOT NULL`; `undefined: no filter`), and `applyVerification`handles the two branches in a single transaction (verify: set`verifiedAt + verifiedByUserId`+ clear`adminNote`if previously rejected; reject: set`adminNote`+ clear`verifiedAt`if previously verified — never touches`deletedAt`/`body`/`title`/`evidenceIpfsCid`/`contentHash`/`ipfsCid`per rule 00). The file enforces a complaint must carry`rating: 1`to satisfy the still-NOT-NULL legacy`rating` column during the ADR-0028 D6 deprecation window (synthesized at the repository boundary not the API boundary so callers don't leak the legacy contract). **M7.3b** (`1d97dc0`, 332 lines) `feat(api): add complaint submit + list use cases and public endpoints`— five files: (a)`application/SubmitComplaintUseCase.ts`(71 lines) builds the IPFS payload with`kind: 'COMPLAINT'`discriminator +`evidenceIpfsCid`field on top of the v2 envelope established in M4.2 (so Phase 3 jury anchoring can reuse the same on-chain`submitReview`pipeline without migration), computes the keccak256`contentHash`deterministically (same hashing as reviews — Phase 3 jury verdict will anchor this hash on-chain), pins to IPFS via`PinataIpfsService`, then delegates to `complaintRepo.create`which atomically writes the row + outbox event. (b)`application/ListComplaintsUseCase.ts`(22 lines) is a thin wrapper around`complaintRepo.list`with explicit method-level docstring noting that the ADR-0029 D4 derived-status filter is the one place anyone should be translating`OPEN/VERIFIED/REJECTED`into DB conditions — clients further up the stack treat the three values as the canonical surface vocabulary. (c)`presentation/routes.ts`(229 lines) ships the public router:`POST /v1/complaints`requires`authMiddleware('reviewer')`(per ADR-0029 D3 only L2+ may file; rule 00 prevents anonymous accusations from contaminating the rule-00-immutable record) + zod body with required`evidenceIpfsCid`(string, IPFS CID shape) + required`brokerSlug`+ required`body`(10-2000 chars) + optional`title`(max 80 chars) + required`sentiment`(per ADR-0028 D4 — complaints carry sentiment so they participate in the broker-detail trust signal).`GET /v1/complaints/broker/:slug`is public-read with optional`?status=OPEN|VERIFIED|REJECTED`filter —`REJECTED`rows ship`adminNote`to the public view per ADR-0029 D4 so anyone can audit why the platform rejected the substantiation.`GET /v1/complaints/:id`is public-read single-fetch. (d)`index.ts`(8 lines) re-exports`complaintsRouter`. (e) `apps/api/src/http/server.ts`mounts`app.route('/v1/complaints', complaintsRouter)` between reviews and admin so existing routing topology stays clean. **M7.3c** (`f1f33cd`, 269 lines) `feat(api): add admin verify/reject endpoints with rule 00 invariant`— two files: (a)`application/VerifyComplaintUseCase.ts` (93 lines) **handles both verify and reject in a single class with a discriminated union input (`kind: 'verify' | 'reject'`)** rather than two parallel use cases — the read-side (load complaint by id + assert `kind === 'COMPLAINT'`+ assert exists) is 60% of the code and would inevitably drift across two separate use cases. The class loads the complaint, validates the action (verify is idempotent — re-verifying just refreshes the`verifiedByUserId`audit trail; admin can also reject a previously-verified complaint, which clears`verifiedAt`while setting`adminNote`so the audit history reflects the reversal), application-layer belt-suspenders re-validates`adminNote.length`is in`[5, 500]`for the reject branch (zod already does this at the route boundary, but defense-in-depth catches future internal callers that bypass the route schema), then delegates to`complaintRepo.applyVerification`which performs the mutation + emits`complaint.verified`or`complaint.rejected`outbox event in the same transaction. (b)`apps/api/src/domains/admin/presentation/routes.ts`adds`GET /admin/complaints`(with`brokerSlug`+ derived`status: 'OPEN'|'VERIFIED'|'REJECTED'|'ALL'`filter; the ALL bucket drops the status filter entirely for historical audit; broker name and author tier hydrated per cursor rule 51 + ADR-0026 three-language ship),`PATCH /admin/complaints/:id/verify`, and `PATCH /admin/complaints/:id/reject`(zod requires`adminNote: z.string().min(5).max(500, { message: '...' })`matching the ADR-0029 D4 mandate). All three endpoints sit under`authMiddleware('admin')`. The cross-domain admin path imports `VerifyComplaintUseCase`from the complaints domain so the URL space stays at the canonical`/v1/admin/complaints/...`per ADR-0029 D4 (vs the deferred-from option of`/v1/complaints/admin/...`which would be a route hierarchy violation with the existing`/v1/admin/users`/`/v1/admin/reviews`/`/v1/admin/verifications`admin URL pattern). The rule-00 invariant ("reject ≠ delete") is encoded in two testable places — the use case validates the discriminated union exhaustively, and the repository's`applyVerification` is the single SQL site that touches these columns. **M7.4** (`1112e9e`, 650 lines) `feat(console): add admin complaint moderation page per ADR-0029`— atomic-but-large per the VerificationsClient (787 lines) precedent: a single admin page with four tightly-coupled internal sub-components (StatusBadge / ComplaintRow / ComplaintDetailModal / RejectReasonModal) where lifting components to separate files would obscure the page's self-contained navigation logic. Seven files: (a)`apps/console/src/lib/api/client.ts`(60 lines insert) adds`fetchAdminComplaints(token, { brokerSlug, status, limit, offset, search })`+`verifyComplaint(token, id)`+`rejectComplaint(token, id, adminNote)`thin client wrappers, plus`AdminComplaintItem`and`AdminComplaintStatus = 'OPEN' | 'VERIFIED' | 'REJECTED'`types matching the API M7.3c shape. (b)`apps/console/src/app/[locale]/admin/complaints/page.tsx`(9 lines) is the route entry — renders`<ComplaintsClient />`. (c) `apps/console/src/app/[locale]/admin/complaints/ComplaintsClient.tsx`(541 lines) is the main client component: (i) StatusBadge differentiates OPEN (amber) / VERIFIED (red — VERIFIED-as-substantiated is a severity escalation in the platform context, not a green "all good" signal — chosen to match how merchant-side triage will read it) / REJECTED (muted slate); (ii) the page header has a 4-state filter (OPEN / VERIFIED / REJECTED / ALL — ALL drops`?status=`from the API call so historical audit is possible) and a search input that filters by broker slug, broker display name, or complaint body excerpt; (iii) ComplaintRow renders broker name (cursor rule 51 + ADR-0026 three-language`localizedBrokerName`helper), author wallet shortened, sentiment badge, body excerpt (clamp-2 lines), age-of-complaint, status badge, and a "View" CTA that opens ComplaintDetailModal; (iv) ComplaintDetailModal shows the full body + title + evidence IPFS link with`target="\_blank"`external link +`rel="noopener"`security pattern, the broker meta panel, the author meta panel (wallet + tier + role), and conditional action buttons — OPEN status shows red "Verify (substantiate)" CTA + grey "Reject" CTA; VERIFIED status shows the verifier admin id + verifiedAt timestamp + a single "Reject (overturn)" CTA that opens RejectReasonModal; REJECTED status shows the adminNote in a readonly callout (rule 00「reject ≠ delete」 — the public-facing reason stays visible) + a "Re-verify (overturn rejection)" CTA; (v) RejectReasonModal is a nested z-70 modal layered above the detail modal that requires a 5-500 char admin note matching the API zod constraint, with client-side validation feedback before submitting. (d)`apps/console/src/components/layout/AuthGate.tsx`adds`/admin/complaints`to the admin nav between Review management and Brokers + an`AlertTriangle`lucide icon. (e-g)`apps/console/messages/{zh-Hant,zh-Hans,en}.json`each gain 17 keys: nav.complaints + admin.complaintsTitle + admin.searchPlaceholder + 4 tab labels + 2 table column headers + admin.noComplaints empty state + 3 status badge labels + admin.complaintVerifyButton + 4 modal section titles + 1 reject button label. Reuses existing`rejectReasonTitle`and a few common labels from the`/admin/verifications`page to avoid duplication. **M7 verification points**: 7/9 commits done; lint-staged + prettier hooks pass on every commit;`pnpm --filter @opentrade/db typecheck`+`pnpm --filter @opentrade/api typecheck`+`pnpm --filter @opentrade/console typecheck`all green (the lone`apps/console`lint warning in`PrivyLoginButton`is pre-existing and unrelated to this session);`POST /v1/complaints`+`GET /v1/complaints/broker/:slug`+`GET /v1/complaints/:id`+`GET /v1/admin/complaints`+`PATCH /v1/admin/complaints/:id/verify`+`PATCH /v1/admin/complaints/:id/reject`six endpoints shipped through`apps/api/src/http/server.ts`; `/admin/complaints`browseable in console (waiting on M7.5 ComplaintForm before a full OPEN→VERIFIED + OPEN→REJECTED smoke test loop is possible). 14-milestone plan progress: still 7/14 milestones (M7 split into 9 sub-commits where 7 are now done) / 31/70 atomic commits. **Next pickup is M7.5**: extract`<EvidenceUpload>`primitive into`packages/ui`(PNG/JPEG/PDF + 5MB cap + Pinata pipeline reuse — the existing`/verify`page hand-rolled upload stays for now, primitive is initially scoped to ComplaintForm) +`apps/web` `ComplaintForm`client component (sentiment from M5`<SentimentPicker>`+ EvidenceUpload + body 10-2000 chars zod validation) + 3-language messages — estimated ~400 lines diff. **Design notes captured for future agents**: (a) M7.1`respondsToReviewId`is column-only without bidirectional Prisma relation — relation wiring waits for M10 broker-response API; this keeps the M7.1 schema commit single-purpose and avoids dragging an unrelated relation into a DB-only commit. (b)`adminNote String? @db.Text`is not in ADR-0029 D1's schema example but D4's reject flow demands it; reusing the`SbtVerificationRequest.adminNote`pattern means console + admin reviewers see the same shape twice in their workflow. (c) M7.3 was split into 3a/3b/3c rather than shipped as a single ~1000-line commit — 3a is unavoidably ~424 lines because the three domain files have circular type dependencies (entity ↔ port ↔ adapter), but 3b (332) + 3c (269) are independently deployable on top of 3a. (d) Admin endpoints live under`/v1/admin/complaints/...`per ADR-0029 D4 spec rather than nested under`/v1/complaints/admin/...`—`VerifyComplaintUseCase`is imported from the complaints domain into the admin domain's presentation layer, which is the established cross-domain pattern (admin domain owns`/v1/admin/users`+`/v1/admin/reviews`+`/v1/admin/verifications`already).
